{timestamp:2026-05-20T03:31:50.005Z,hook_event_name:PreToolUse,session_id:02612266-1b95-4e3d-a098-ed17df047337,transcript_path:c:\\Users\\matej\\AppData\\Roaming\\Code\\User\\workspaceStorage\\271b9a8906553d5139d4e30a74207f5e\\GitHub.copilot-chat\\transcripts\\02612266-1b95-4e3d-a098-ed17df047337.jsonl,tool_name:runSubagent,tool_input:{agentName:Coda,description:Fix Edit POST to use fetch-then-map pattern,prompt:Fix the Edit POST actions in four controllers in the Carnivorous Plant Nursery ASP.NET Core MVC project to use the safe fetch-then-map pattern described in Lab4.\n\n## The problem\nAll four Edit POST actions currently do this:\n```csharp\npublic IActionResult Edit(int id, Plant model) // model comes directly from form POST\n{\n _plantRepository.Update(model); // blindly replaces entire DB row\n}\n```\n`_db.Plant.Update(model)` marks ALL properties as modified, including `DeletedAt`. Since `DeletedAt` is never on the form, it comes back as `null`, which would clear a soft-delete timestamp if the form were submitted against a record. This is the over-posting / mass-assignment problem Lab4 warns about.\n\n## The fix GÇö fetch-then-map pattern\nEach Edit POST must:\n1. Fetch the live entity from the DB (via the repository `GetById` GÇö which already filters `DeletedAt == null`, so a deleted record returns `null` GĺĆ `NotFound`)\n2. Map only the user-editable fields from the posted form model onto the fetched entity\n3. Validate `ModelState.IsValid` (after mapping, so the view gets the properly-populated entity on failure)\n4. Call `Update` with the fetched entity (not the form model)\n\nThis means `DeletedAt`, `Id`, and any other system-managed fields are never touched by the form.\n\n---\n\n## Read these files first\n- {timestamp:2026-05-20T03:31:52.520Z,hook_event_name:UserPromptSubmit,session_id:02612266-1b95-4e3d-a098-ed17df047337,transcript_path:c:\\Users\\matej\\AppData\\Roaming\\Code\\User\\workspaceStorage\\271b9a8906553d5139d4e30a74207f5e\\GitHub.copilot-chat\\transcripts\\02612266-1b95-4e3d-a098-ed17df047337.jsonl,prompt:Fix the Edit POST actions in four controllers in the Carnivorous Plant Nursery ASP.NET Core MVC project to use the safe fetch-then-map pattern described in Lab4.\n\n## The problem\nAll four Edit POST actions currently do this:\n```csharp\npublic IActionResult Edit(int id, Plant model) // model comes directly from form POST\n{\n _plantRepository.Update(model); // blindly replaces entire DB row\n}\n```\n`_db.Plant.Update(model)` marks ALL properties as modified, including `DeletedAt`. Since `DeletedAt` is never on the form, it comes back as `null`, which would clear a soft-delete timestamp if the form were submitted against a record. This is the over-posting / mass-assignment problem Lab4 warns about.\n\n## The fix GÇö fetch-then-map pattern\nEach Edit POST must:\n1. Fetch the live entity from the DB (via the repository `GetById` GÇö which already filters `DeletedAt == null`, so a deleted record returns `null` GĺĆ `NotFound`)\n2. Map only the user-editable fields from the posted form model onto the fetched entity\n3. Validate `ModelState.IsValid` (after mapping, so the view gets the properly-populated entity on failure)\n4. Call `Update` with the fetched entity (not the form model)\n\nThis means `DeletedAt`, `Id`, and any other system-managed fields are never touched by the form.\n\n---\n\n## Read these files first\n- Has a visible text input (what the user types into)\n2. Has a hidden input with `name="searchTerm"` (what gets submitted in the form)\n3. On each keystroke (debounced 300ms), fires an AJAX request to `/plants/suggestions?term=XXX`\n4. Shows a dropdown list of suggestions below the input GÇö `text` is displayed, `value` is what goes into the hidden input and the visible input on selection\n6. Supports keyboard navigation (GĺćGĺô to move, Enter to select, Escape to close)\n7. Clicking outside closes the dropdown\n8. When a suggestion is selected: fill the visible input with `value`, fill the hidden input with `value`, close the dropdown, and submit the parent `<form>` automatically\n9. If the user manually clears the input, the hidden input is also cleared\n10. On page load, if the hidden input already has a value (pre-filled from model/ViewBag), the visible input should show that value too\n11. Minimum 1 character to trigger AJAX\n\n## Styling Requirements\n\nMust match the existing nursery theme.
